                $(this).datepicker({
                    autoFocusNextInput: true,
                    constrainInput: false,
                    changeMonth: true,
                    changeYear: true,
                    beforeShow: function(input, inst) { $('#ui-datepicker-div').addClass('show'); },

                var format = $(this).data('format') || 'mm/dd';

                    autoFocusNextInput: true,
                    constrainInput: false,
                    changeMonth: true,
                    changeYear: false,

                    maxDate: new Date(d.getFullYear(), 12-1, 31),
